define i8* @get_topic() {
entry:
  %topic_ptr = alloca i8*, align 8
  %topic_load = load i8*, i8** %topic_ptr, align 8
  %0 = icmp eq i8* %topic_load, null
  br i1 %0, label %then, label %else

then:                                             ; preds = %entry
  %1 = call i8* @str()
  ret i8* %1

else:                                             ; preds = %entry
  %empty_str_load = load i8*, [1 x i8]* @.empty_str, align 8
  ret i8* %empty_str_load

merge:                                            ; No predecessors!
  ret void
}
